	}
}

	MAX_APPLY
	PROB_MUTATE_CODEBLOCK

		TEXT_LINE
	}
}

	ORGANISM_ID
	X
	Y
	MOOD
	MESSAGE

	MACHINE {
		TERMINATED
		CB
		PC
		R[N] {
			VALUE
		}

			PC
		}

			VALUE
		}
	}
}

	}

	VALUE
}

		Y
	}
}

	HEIGHT
